`FeedFilters.includeCeremonial?: boolean` and `SponsorFilters.includeCeremonial?: boolean` flow through `buildFeedWhere` / `buildSponsorWhere`. Both helpers append `(is_ceremonial = 0 OR is_ceremonial IS NULL)` unless the flag is true. NULL counts as visible during backfill so the dashboard doesn't go dark while the classifier is running. The flag becomes part of the `unstable_cache` argument-derived key, so the on/off variants live in separate cache slots.

Don't apply on `/watchlist` or `/bill/[id]` — watched ceremonial bills must surface, and detail pages always render. The toggle is a list-view concept. `getFeedStats(includeCeremonial, cluster?)`, `getSponsorRecentBills(key, includeCeremonial)`, `getSponsorStats(key, includeCeremonial)`, and `getSponsorTopTopics(key, limit, includeCeremonial)` all take the flag explicitly so the expanded sponsor panel matches the active toggle.

### Cluster filter (`?cluster=<slug>`)

Regex-based template clustering. Patterns + `classifyCluster(title, billType)` live in `lib/cluster-patterns.ts` (single source of truth — pattern revision is cheap because there's no separate metadata store). The sync upsert calls `classifyCluster` unconditionally on every bill (pure regex, zero cost) and writes `cluster_id` in the same `INSERT ... ON CONFLICT` statement.

`FeedFilters.cluster?: string` propagates through `buildFeedWhere`, which adds `cluster_id = ?`. **Cluster bypasses the ceremonial gate** — when `cluster` is set, `buildFeedWhere` skips the `(is_ceremonial = 0 OR is_ceremonial IS NULL)` clause entirely. Reasoning: most clusters are mostly ceremonial; opting into "awareness designations" means asking to see the noise. The toggle is suppressed in `HeaderBar` whenever `feedFilters.cluster` is set so the dead control isn't rendered.

Sponsor queries do not take the cluster filter (sponsor page is about people, not bill shapes). `getClusterStats()` returns `[{id, name, description, count, exampleTitle}]` sorted by count desc; `getUnmatchedClusterCount(includeCeremonial)` returns `COUNT(*) WHERE cluster_id IS NULL` honoring the active ceremonial filter. Both cached `tags: ["bills"]`.

Backfill: `npm run backfill-clusters` → `scripts/backfill-clusters.ts`. Pure regex, no API calls; runs in under a minute against the full corpus. Idempotent via `WHERE cluster_id IS NULL` so re-running after adding a sixth pattern only touches previously-unmatched rows. Logs per-cluster counts at the end. POSTs to `REVALIDATE_URL` (with `Authorization: Bearer ${CRON_SECRET}`) on completion to invalidate the `bills` tag, same as the ceremonial backfill.

### Feed sort (`?sort=action|introduced`)

Applies to `/` and `/watchlist` only. Two keys, default `action`:

- `action`: `ORDER BY latest_action_date DESC NULLS LAST, id DESC`
- `introduced`: `ORDER BY introduced_date DESC NULLS LAST, id DESC`

`SortDropdown` is a client component that mirrors `StageFilter`. It deletes `expanded` and (for the default) `sort` from the URL on change, preserves everything else. The visible Action column always shows `latest_action_date` regardless of sort key — the sort axis isn't what's displayed.

Do **not** add the dropdown to `/stale` (forced ASC by definition) or `/members` (sorted by `bill_count`, different axis). The `/bills?stage=president` alias keeps the dropdown — picking an explicit `?sort` there is exactly what disables the desk-time/ASC alias path.

`FeedFilters` includes an optional `sponsor?: string`. When set, `buildFeedWhere` ANDs `sponsor_name = ?` so `/?sponsor=<encoded name>` filters the main feed. The HeaderBar count line shows `· sponsored by <name>` in `--accent-amber` when active. All other feed filters (stage, topics, q) compose with it via the same plumbing — and the `StageFilter`, `TopicFilter`, `BillRow` components all thread `sponsor` through their generated hrefs, same way they thread `q`.

## Summarization prompt

Keep summaries 2-3 sentences. Plain English. Neutral. Focus on what the bill *does*, not what it's titled. The CRS summary is a useful input but should not be copied.

Prompt template:

```
You are summarizing a US Congress bill for a personal tracking dashboard. Write a 2-3 sentence summary in plain English that explains what the bill would actually change if enacted. Avoid legalese, avoid the bill's marketing title, avoid editorial language. State who is affected and how.

Then output a JSON block with:
- topics: array of 1-3 topic tags from this list: [healthcare, immigration, taxes, defense, energy, environment, education, labor, technology, civil_rights, criminal_justice, agriculture, trade, housing, transportation, foreign_policy, veterans, elections, budget, financial_services, government_operations, consumer_protection, social_security, other]
- is_ceremonial: true if symbolic (awareness days, building renamings, recognitions, sense-of-Congress); false if it changes law, appropriates funds, or directs an agency

Bill title: {title}
Latest action: {latest_action_text}
CRS summary (if any): {crs_summary}
Bill text (truncated): {bill_text_first_8000_chars}

Respond in this exact format:

SUMMARY:
<2-3 sentences>

JSON:
{"topics": [...], "is_ceremonial": true|false}
```

**The prompt does NOT emit `stage` (HO 386).** `stage` is owned entirely by `computeStage(latest_action_text)` (HO 383, sole authority; coverage rules extended HO 385) — the LLM's stage field was generated-parsed-discarded dead weight and was removed from the prompt, the JSON shape, and the parse. The summarize JSON contract is now `{topics, is_ceremonial}`; the runner derives + writes stage from `computeStage` independently.

Parse the response by splitting on `JSON:` and parsing the second half. If parsing fails, log the bill ID and skip it; don't crash the sync. The `is_ceremonial` field is defensive: if the model omits it or returns a non-boolean, the parser writes NULL so the standalone backfill (`npm run classify-ceremonial`) can pick it up later. Title-only re-classification lives in `lib/classify-ceremonial.ts`; the sync `UPSERT_SQL` clears `is_ceremonial` along with `summary` whenever `update_date` changes so re-classification rides through the inline summarize path with no extra Gemini call.

The prompt will need iteration. Expect to revise it 5-10 times. Common failure modes: LLM repeats the bill's marketing title, LLM editorializes, LLM picks `other` for the topic when a better tag exists. Test against a sample of 20 known bills and read the outputs side by side.

### Stage-monotonicity guard (HO 239)

`stage` is computed deterministically from `latest_action_text` by `computeStage` (`lib/enums.ts`) — the sole authority since HO 383; the LLM no longer classifies stage (its dead stage output was removed in HO 386). Two guards keep `stage` monotonic — it only advances:

- **Compute-side** (`computeStage`, `lib/enums.ts`): the ordered action-text→stage ladder (enacted → president → other_chamber → floor → committee → introduced, first match wins) plus the embedded guard (b) — post-passage procedural actions like "motion to reconsider laid on the table" mean the chamber already acted, so classify `floor`, never `introduced`/`committee`. HO 385 extended the ladder to cover the patterns the old LLM stage implicitly caught (cross-chamber receipt → other_chamber; "agreed to"/cloture/suspension/"held at the desk" → floor; calendar placement/hearings/subcommittee/markup/discharge → committee; private law → enacted), closing all but a documented ~124-row residual of cases uncatchable from latest-action text alone. **Floor-rung semantics:** `floor` = passed/voted-on a chamber's floor, so calendar placement (reported-out, awaiting a floor vote) maps to `committee`, not `floor`. Guard (a) — never regress once advanced — is enforced code-side, not here.
- **Code-side** (`lib/summarize-runner.ts::decideStage(current, proposed, pending)` → `"advance" | "reject" | "pend" | "noop"`): ranks via `stageRank` (`lib/enums.ts` — `ALLOWED_STAGES.indexOf`, introduced=0 … enacted=5, unlisted/null=−1). `proposed` ahead of `current` → **advance**, the ONLY path that writes `stage`/`previous_stage`/`stage_changed_at` and appends a `stage_transitions` row. A downgrade **to `introduced`** → **reject** (impossible regression; keeps the old stage, clears any pending, logs `[stage] rejected impossible downgrade`). Any **other** downgrade → **pend**: parked in `pending_stage`/`pending_stage_at`, and the slot does NOT move until a SECOND matching proposal confirms it (`proposed === pending` → advance) — a two-tick vote so one noisy classification can't drag a bill backward. `noop` when unchanged or first-seen-`introduced`. On anything but `advance`, nothing touches `stage`/`previous_stage`/`stage_changed_at`/`stage_transitions`.

## Dashboard lead generation

The dashboard's top-of-page `DashboardLead` is a 3-sentence prose summary, generated once per cron tick by `lib/dashboard-lead.ts::generateDashboardLead`.

> **ORPHANED RENDER as of HO 244.** The masthead became a stat readout (`n bills tracked · …`), so nothing renders this lead anymore — but the cron **still generates and stores it every tick** (`getDashboardLead` is the deprecated-candidate read; see Query helpers). The generator below is intact; retiring it vs. re-homing the one-liner is a pending design call. Don't delete the pipeline.

- **Inputs:** corpus size, last-7-day stage transitions (count + top 5 with bill ID, truncated title, transition arrow), last-7-day enactments (count + top 3 IDs), last-7-day new introductions (count), and the topic with the most transitions in the last 7 days. All gathered by focused queries in `lib/dashboard-lead.ts` — not cached UI helpers.
- **Model:** `gemini-2.5-flash`, single completion, reuses the `SUMMARY_MODEL` constant and client pattern from `lib/summarize.ts`.
- **Prompt** lives in source under `lib/dashboard-lead.ts`. Expect prompt iteration over the first 5-10 generations — same failure modes as the summarize prompt (marketing-title creep, generic openers like "This week, Congress...", vague numbers, editorial framing).
- **Storage:** upserted into `dashboard_state` under `key = 'weekly_lead'` with a JS-side ISO `updated_at`. Read back by `getDashboardLead()`.
- **Cron integration:** `app/api/sync/route.ts` calls `generateDashboardLead` + `writeDashboardLead` after sync + summarize, then `revalidateTag("bills")`. Failure is non-fatal — the cron logs a warning, the prior lead stays in the DB, and the dashboard keeps rendering it.
- **Manual run:** `npm run lead` → `scripts/generate-lead.ts` generates, prints, and writes a lead. Use it to iterate on the prompt without waiting for cron.

## Report generation

Weekly reports — one Markdown blob per calendar week, rendered at `/reports/[slug]`.

- Generated weekly on Monday 09:30 UTC by `app/api/cron/weekly-report/route.ts`, which calls `lib/report-generation.ts::generateWeeklyReport`. HO 139 split this out of `/api/sync` after the shared Monday 09:00 tick repeatedly never reached the report step inside its 60s budget; the route now has the full ceiling to itself and the cron is Monday-only via the `30 9 * * 1` schedule.
- **Incomplete-week guard (HO 110):** `generateWeeklyReport` throws if `week.end` is in the future, so a report is never generated for a week that hasn't closed (the cron treats the throw as non-fatal and retries next tick). The 2026-05-18 backfilled row predates the guard and is left as a historical artifact.
- One Gemini call per report. Structured output with four section markers (`LEAD`, `STAGE_COMMENTARY`, `ENACTMENTS_COMMENTARY`, `MOST_TALKED_COMMENTARY`). Parsed by splitting on markers, same pattern as the summarize prompt. The `ENACTMENTS_COMMENTARY` and `STAGE_COMMENTARY` slots also carry the LLM's zero-count placeholder, though assembly owns the copy when a count is zero and ignores the LLM output there.
- The Markdown body is assembled programmatically: section headers + counts come from the data, prose comes from the LLM. Bill IDs render as plain text (`HR 2702`); stage transitions use the canonical `▸ INTRO → ▸▸ COMMITTEE` glyphs.
- Storage: upserted into `reports` keyed by `slug` (the ISO week-start date). Re-running for the same week overwrites the prior row.
- Failure mode: cron logs a warning and writes no row; the sync's other steps still complete. Manual recovery: `npm run report` (prior week) or `npm run report YYYY-MM-DD` (specific week start). `scripts/generate-report.ts` prints the assembled Markdown before writing — useful for iterating on the prompt.
- Notable introductions ranks by `cosponsor_count DESC NULLS LAST`, tiebroken by `COALESCE(text_length, 0) DESC` then `id DESC`. The pre-filter `(text_length IS NULL OR text_length > 5000)` excludes short resolutions and one-pagers that slip past the ceremonial+cluster gates while keeping NULL rows visible during backfill. CRA-disapproval is included as substantive; other clusters are filtered out. (The handoff-58 `LENGTH(summary)` proxy was retired in handoff 59.)
- Markdown rendered on `/reports/[slug]` via `react-markdown` + `remark-gfm` (needed for the topic-breakdown table) with terminal-aesthetic component overrides in `components/ReportMarkdown.tsx`.
- Bill IDs in a rendered report auto-link to `/bill/[id]` (HO 113): `ReportMarkdown` pre-substitutes bare IDs (`HR 2702`, `HJRES 140`, …) into markdown links before rendering, normalizing to the `{getCurrentCongress()}-{type}-{number}` `bills.id` form. A `[`-lookbehind prevents double-wrapping an already-linked ID; `(?!\d)` leaves a trailing `'s`/`s` outside the link.
- "Most talked about" is confidence-gated (HO 111): the `mostTalkedAbout` query keeps only `news_mentions` rows with `match_confidence >= 0.7` (which also excludes NULL-confidence rows — SQL three-valued logic), and only bills with `>= 2` such mentions. Ranked by mention count → avg confidence → recency. The prompt context gets a bucketed `confidence_tier` (`high` >= 0.9, else `medium`) plus outlets and sample headlines — never the raw float.
- The prose prompt (`SYSTEM_PROMPT` in `lib/report-generation.ts`, tuned HO 112) enforces a synthesis-not-recite LEAD, an anti-restate rule (prose states a section's significance, not the list's contents), confidence-tier verb guidance, no LLM-invented counts, and a banned-phrase list. `buildUserPrompt` feeds week-over-week introduction deltas and per-transition direction (forward/backward) as synthesis raw material. Gemini 2.5 Flash obeys imperfectly — banned-word inflections still leak occasionally; further LEAD tuning is HO 112.1 territory.

### Report section anatomy (HO 352 / 358 / 360)

The body assembly (`buildReportMarkdown` in `lib/report-generation.ts`) carries two structured sections worth knowing the shape of, **in this order**:

- **Stage movements** (`## Stage movements (N)`) renders as a **destination-stage ladder** (HO 352) — one rung per stage in canonical order (`LADDER_STAGES`; **`introduced` is NOT a rung** — a fresh intro has no "advance into" story), sqrt-scaled bars reusing the dashboard stage-distribution bar, zero-count rungs kept dimmed. The **committee** rung is routine referrals, **count-only**; rungs past committee (floor+) name their bills on sub-lines, capped with a `+N more` tail (`rung.billTotal − rung.bills.length`). This replaced the old per-transition row list.
- **Floor votes** (`## Floor votes (N)`) sits **after** Stage movements (the natural read: what moved, then how the floor voted). Named decisive votes are one line each (`formatVoteLine`): **bold outcome verb** `PASSED / FAILED / ADVANCED / BLOCKED / CONFIRMED / REJECTED` · chamber `S`/`H` · bill ref (a **bare ID** like `HR 2702`, linkified to `/bill/119-…` by `ReportMarkdown`'s `linkifyBillIds`, **NOT** `/bills/slug`) or `nominee → position` · margin `yea–nay` (cloture-prefixed for ADVANCED/BLOCKED) · party split (`D y–n · R y–n`, with `I` only when notable) shown **only on contested/divergent** votes (`shouldShowSplit` — diverging parties or a tight margin). The verb classifier (`classifyVote`) reads live `result` / `question` / `amendment_designation` — no invented strings. Procedural / amendment / UC-nomination votes collapse to a `+ N more recorded vote(s)` line. Recess states are handled (`formatRecessLine`: one-chamber-dark line; both-in-session-no-votes; both-in-recess).
- **`content_md` is one pure-markdown string.** The web render (`ReportMarkdown`) and the `.md` download are identical **except one deliberate web-only divergence**: `ReportMarkdown` colors the outcome verb by **exact-text match** on the bolded token (`PASSED`/`CONFIRMED` → `--stage-enacted`; `ADVANCED` → `--stage-floor`; `FAILED`/`BLOCKED`/`REJECTED` → `--party-republican`); every other `<strong>` stays `--text-secondary`, so a bolded prose word never false-matches. The stored markdown carries **no color/HTML** — just `**FAILED**` — so the download is plain bold. (See oddities for why color can't live in `content_md`, and that the same rule could later re-color the 352 ladder's stage labels.)

## Frontend design system

Bloomberg Terminal aesthetic. Dark monospace, dense rows, color-coded stages and topics. No light mode. **Typeface rule — mono for chrome, sans for prose (HO 299/300):** the app is monospace by default, but the **`--sans` token** (`system-ui, -apple-system, "Segoe UI", Roboto, sans-serif`) is now used for **PROSE in the v2 feed** — bill titles, summaries, news headlines, sponsor names. **Mono stays for ALL chrome** — chips, metrics, labels, IDs, dates, anything coded. This is the **first sans in CBT** (older comments in `globals.css` still say "no `--sans` in CBT" — stale, predate the token); the convention now reads "mono for chrome, sans for prose," not mono-only. Tailwind v4 only (no shadcn / no other libraries). Server components by default. Client islands are now numerous (~53 `"use client"` components — 55 `^"use client"` grep matches under `components/` incl. the 2 hook files `useSingleOpenPanel.ts` / `use-watch-toggle.ts`; **HO 328 added `CommitteeRailRow` + `RosterShowAll` (the `/members` rail rows + roster disclosure) and deleted `MemberProductivityScatter`** with the scatter; earlier: `CartogramShell` / `RaceMapCard` / `PrimaryMapCard` added HO 210) — filter/URL chips (`StageFilter`, `PartyFilter`, `StateFilter`, `CeremonialToggle`, `SortDropdown`, `SearchBox`, `SearchTabs`), the feed + dashboard accordions (`BillRowList` / `BillRow` / `BillExpandedPanel` / `TopStallsList`), interactive charts (`DashboardTopicTreemap`, `StageFunnel`; the `/patterns` `PatternBars` ranked-bar list that replaced `PatternBubbleSVG` in HO 347 is a **server** component — URL-driven `<Link>` rows, not an island), chrome (`MarketsTapeClient`, `CyclingTimestamp`, `ActivityTabs`, `Tooltip`, `MobileNavDrawer` — dormant), and row affordances (`WatchlistToggle`, `WatchStar`, `MediaAttentionCell`, `MemberHeader`, `RaceIncumbentCard`, `StateFlag`, `SponsorPhoto`, `SponsorHoverName`). See `### Server / client split` for the canonical set.

### Pages

- `/dashboard-classic` — **HO 311: TEMPORARY** — the former `/` dashboard, preserved verbatim at this unlinked route (no nav entry; direct URL only) for one cycle as the v2-swap comparison + no-git-undo surface; sunset in a later handoff (open loop). Post-swap its three click-to-filter components take `basePath="/dashboard-classic"` so the funnel / treemap / `× CLEAR` rebase THIS route instead of pushing to `/` (now v2, which ignores the params); the non-gated `getCorpusStats` count and the filtered feed are otherwise the old `/` unchanged. Original description: dashboard (HO 131 foundation, evolved through HO 133/134/132/149/**150**). HO 150 reflowed the layout per spec 1. **`HomeHeader`** chrome-stacks: (1) **masthead** (single-column full-width as of HO 162; **HO 185 replaced the brand prompt with the unified breadcrumb path**) — line 1 pairs the **brand path** `Congressional Terminal:\119TH\Dashboard>` (shared `BreadcrumbMasthead`; segment text `--text-primary`, the `:\` `\` `>` glyphs `--accent-amber`, tight shell spacing) with a **STAT READOUT** (HO 244, **replacing HO 178's prose LEAD**): `n bills tracked · n in committee · n on the floor · n other chamber · n enacted`. **HO 244 dropped the brand from the 36px HO 162 hero to 20px mono** (word-spacing −6px) so the readout fits baseline-aligned after it. Readout color tokens (`.stat-total/-committee/-floor/-other/-enacted` in `HomeHeader`): total = `--party-democrat`, committee = `--party-republican`, floor = `--accent-amber-bright`, other chamber = `--stage-other-chamber`, enacted = `--stage-enacted`. A single blinking `_` caret (`--accent-amber-bright`, **desktop-only**) rides the **readout's end** (`.home-readout-caret`); `BreadcrumbMasthead` renders `cursor={false}` so the path carries none. Exactly one caret. The caret is **one of three named motion exceptions** alongside the tape marquee and the HO 183 cycling timestamps. **DO-NOT-RECONCILE:** COMMITTEE reads **red** here (`--party-republican`) but stays **cyan** as a bar in the distributions panel (`--stage-committee`) — an accepted mismatch, do not "fix" it. (2) the `· LAST SYNC h:MM AM/PM <ZONE>` meta line (11px `--text-muted`, dim; 12-hour as of HO 169; **HO 244 moved `N BILLS TRACKED` up into the readout total** and the line is no longer pinned far-right; the time token still CYCLES zones ET→CT→MT→PT→UTC as of HO 183 via `CyclingTimestamp` — see "Date formatting" / the third motion exception); (3) **a single combined markets tape** (`<MarketsTape />`, HO 234 collapsed the HO 178 dual `.markets-tape-block` pair to one line — see "Markets tape") between the masthead block and the nav; (4) **full-width nav** — seven `NAV_ITEMS` (Dashboard · Legislation · Members · Electoral · Patterns · Reports · Watchlist; **HO 230 restyled it to the text-only path style** — `\`-prefixed items, bracketed active item, 3-group dividers, no icons — and the `Bills|News` label became `Bills`, **then the `Legislation` display label in HO 362 — route stays `/bills`, the `feed` nav key + `bills` mode value unchanged; the breadcrumb crumb, the `BILLS|NEWS` mode toggle, and the `/search` category tab all read "Legislation" too**); active state amber-bright + 2px amber underline. Reports is a top-level entry as of HO 150; `pathToNavKey("/reports")` is special-cased to return `"reports"`. HO 154.5 extended `pathToNavKey` with prefix matchers so every dynamic-segment detail route highlights the right top-nav tab: `/bill/*` → Bills (key `feed`), `/members/*` / `/committee/*` → Members, **`/races` + `/race/*` → Races**, and **`/primaries` → Races** too — **HO 173** split Races + Primaries out of the Members group into their own **`races` GROUP_TABS sub-nav group**, so `/races` and `/primaries` now render the electoral sub-strip (**Races · Primaries**) and both light the Races top-nav tab; the Members group shrank to **Members · Committees**, then to a **single Members tab** in HO 328 when `/committees` folded into the `/members` rail. The group key is `"races"` (not `"electoral"`) so it unifies with the existing top-nav `races` NavItem — `pathToNavKey`'s group loop returns `"races"` for both `/races` and `/primaries` with no extra matcher (the explicit prefix matcher only catches `/race/[id]` detail). `/reports/*` → Reports. Each detail page now passes its actual URL as `basePath` to HeaderBar (e.g. `<HeaderBar basePath={/bill/${bill.id}} />`). The first entry `⌂ DASHBOARD` (HO 140) is amber-highlighted on this page. **HO 162 moved the STAGES + TOPICS legend out of the masthead** (killing the wide-viewport void — no tall right-rail driving row height); **HO 167 then split it into per-chart keys** — `StageKey` and `TopicKey` render the swatch rows (`.panel-key`) at the **top of their own panels** (under the panel label, above the chart body), so each key sits with the chart it decodes. The interim HO 162 footer (`.home-footer` / `.color-key-footer` / the `ColorKeyStrip` component) was **retired** in HO 167. (The `?` `LegendBadge` that briefly held the PARTIES / BILL TYPES / ACCENT reference was **removed in HO 179.1** — the party-dot / bill-type meanings read as self-evident; its function was deleted from `ColorKeyStrip`, which then exported only `StageKey`/`TopicKey`.) **HO 244 retired the rest:** the distributions-merge dropped the key rows, so `StageKey`/`TopicKey`, `ColorKeyStrip.tsx`, and `lib/color-key.ts` are all **deleted** — purge any reference. **HO 244–246 reflowed the body top-to-bottom** (superseding the HO 178 "races in the right column, 56/44, ReportSnapshot+EnactedBanner banners above the grid" layout). The new order under the chrome stack is: **RACES PANEL full-width → WEEKLY BAND full-width (a divider rule above it) → a two-column body**. The HO 233 `RacesPanelTabs` (COMPETITIVE · PRIMARIES tabs, ActivityTabs idiom; COMPETITIVE default — PRIMARIES renders a 6-month timeline strip + the soonest-date cards + an `ALL PRIMARIES →` expander via `DashboardPrimaries`/the uncached `getDashboardPrimaries` rollup, pre-results, no ShareBar/★) now spans **full width** at the top of the body. **The panel chrome (`.home-races-pane`, the popover containment box) lives in `RacesPanelTabs`** (moved out of `CompetitiveRacesStrip` in HO 233 — `CompetitiveRacesStrip` renders only the card grid); a `.races-panel-body` min-height holds both tabs at the same height (no column jump). Below the races panel sits the full-width **`WeeklyBand`** (HO 244 — see its note below, replacing the deleted `<ReportSnapshot />` + `EnactedBanner`). Below that, the **`.home-grid` is `56fr 44fr` (16px gutter)**: **LEFT column (56%)** stacks BREAKING → the tabbed DISTRIBUTIONS panel; **RIGHT column (44%)** is the MOVERS / TOP STALLS feed. **BREAKING is now compact rows** (`BreakingRow`: ID · truncated headline · age) with a hover-expand overlay that overruns rightward into the RIGHT column (the MOVERS / TOP STALLS feed — `.home-grid:has(.breaking-row:hover) .home-col-right`; **post-HO-244 the right column is MOVERS, not the races panel it was under HO 178**) and dims it to 0.4 via CSS `:has()` (replaced the `showFullHeadline` full-width strip; the long-headline cross-column overrun is structurally in place but **not yet visually confirmed on a long-enough headline** — a deferred follow-up). **Competitive races are a responsive card grid with a ticker-style hover popover** (`CompetitiveRacesStrip`, now a **server** component — the HO 166/170 click-to-expand confined drawer + `useSingleOpenPanel` are retired). **HO 245 made the grid full-width-responsive — 4-up ≥1200px, 2-up 700–1199px, 1-up <700px** (was the HO 178 2×2; balanced rows, no 3+1 wrap). The HO 230 hover-popover confinement is keyed to the 2×2 by index, so the **≥1200 single-row path overrides it in CSS** (the popover escapes the pane, opens downward, horizontal direction re-derived from `nth-child`); the 2-up / 1-up paths keep the original 2×2 confinement. Each card is a `<Link>` → `/race/[id]`, and hovering reveals an absolute, opaque (`--bg-row-hover`) popover rendering `RaceHubBody` in **`preview`** mode from **server-prefetched** hub data (no client `/api/race/[id]/hub` fetch; the endpoint is left in place, unused by this surface). Senate-led mix (top 2 Senate + top 2 House by competitiveness via `getMostCompetitiveRaces`); each card = seat label (carries HOUSE/SENATE) + incumbent (party dot + name, "OPEN SEAT" when null) + topline multi-source `RatingChip size="sm"`. **STAGE + TOPIC distributions are now ONE tabbed panel (`DistributionsTabs`, HO 244)** — tabs **STAGE DISTRIBUTION | TOPIC DISTRIBUTION**, with a **fixed ~230px content height** so the bars stay dense and the tab swap doesn't jump; the treemap redraws to the panel's actual w×h. STAGE stays bars (the `StageFunnel`; committee ~91% / president 0 makes a treemap one blob plus slivers — rejected); TOPIC stays a squarified treemap (`DashboardTopicTreemap`, HO 231 — it REPLACED the HO 128/132 d3-pack bubble cluster; `DashboardBubbleChart` **deleted**), area-honest, GOV-anchored, colors from `lib/topic-colors.ts`, the `?topics=` click-to-filter intact (HO 180 per-topic colors + hover popover carry over). **The merge dropped the legend/key row entirely** — the HO 167 `StageKey` / `TopicKey` `.panel-key` rows are gone, and with them `ColorKeyStrip.tsx` + `lib/color-key.ts` (both **deleted**). The RIGHT column's `ActivityTabs` — **its left tab was renamed ACTIVITY → MOVERS in place (HO 232; label/identifier/aria only, predicate unchanged: `getStageChanges`, 7d, recency)**, so the tabs are now MOVERS default + TOP STALLS — **HO 164 made both tabs' rows click-to-expand into the full `BillExpandedPanel`** (summary + meta instant, committees/news on fetch, action chips), single-open within each tab and reset-on-switch (the inactive tab unmounts); ACTIVITY renders `<BillRowList compact>`, TOP STALLS keeps its `[chip][title][Xd]` layout via the new `TopStallsList` wrapper. The HO 131/133/134 no-scroll `height: calc(100vh - var(--home-header-height) - 24px)` is gone — the dashboard scrolls if content exceeds viewport (a conscious reversal so the bubbles can read at full half-width per spec 1; answer-above-fold is preserved by masthead+tape+BREAKING). **HO 244 replaced the HO 153 `<ReportSnapshot />` band with the full-width `WeeklyBand`** (`ReportSnapshot.tsx` deleted). The `WeeklyBand` is a **one-line metrics strip, middot-separated** (HO 365 layout refresh — was pipe-separated) — `Week of <MON DD> · ● n ENACTED · S n · n NEW BILLS · n STAGE TRANSITIONS · n HEARINGS · filler n% · <MON DD> report →` — that folds the former standalone `EnactedBanner` into the `● n ENACTED · S n` segment, carries the HO 351 `filler n%` share bar in-run, and ends with a **dated** `<MON DD> report →` link (HO 365, was `READ FULL →`) into the most recent **finalized** weekly report. It sits full-width between the races panel and the 56/44 grid (a divider rule above it). **B5 (HO 283/286/365):** each of the four **count** metrics (ENACTED / NEW BILLS / STAGE TRANSITIONS / HEARINGS) carries a **WoW delta** (`▲`/`▼`/`±0`, the tape's `--market-up`/`--market-down`/`--text-dim` tokens) AND — as of **HO 365** — a **rich hover card** (`components/WeeklyBandMetricCard.tsx`: a static card PORTALED to `<body>` via `lib/tooltip-position.ts` to escape the dashboard's overflow-clip; **replaced** the flat HO 284 `MetricTip` popover) showing a **sparkline** + a per-metric breakdown. **FILLER carries no card** (HO 351 share bar). **HEARINGS is the fourth metric (HO 286)** — a trailing-7-day committee-meeting count (held meetings only). **Window semantics — the durable rule (HO 365):** the four counts AND their deltas are computed over a **trailing-7-day** window `[now-7d, now)` (via `getWeeklyBandPriorWeek` / `getWeeklyBandHearings.priorWeek` / the headline helpers), comparing trailing-7d vs the prior trailing-7d; the `Week of <MON DD>` label is a human header over that rolling window, **NOT** a calendar (Mon–Sun) boundary. Do not re-implement as calendar week-to-date — partial-week-vs-full-week reads ▼ every day until Sunday, a daily false "down" signal (this misfired from a mock in HO 365; see oddities). **Data:** `getEnactedThisWeek` (count + first ≤3 IDs), `getStageChangesCount({},7)`, `getNewBillsThisWeekCount`, **`getWeeklyBandHearings` (this+prior week, tag `meetings`), `getWeeklyBandPriorWeek` (the three bills-metric prior-week counterparts, tag `bills`)** for the deltas, plus `getDashboardReportSnapshot()` for the dated `<MON DD> report →` target (`snap.latest` → `/reports/{slug}`, label `weekStart`; the most recent **finalized** report — never "this week's", there is no mid-week report). The five HO 365 hover-card breakdown helpers (`getWeeklyBandTransitionLadder` / `getWeeklyBandNewBillsBreakdown` / `getWeeklyBandHearingBreakdown` / `getWeeklyBandHistory` / `getMostRecentEnacted`) back the rich cards — see Query helpers. **Renders on both `/` and `/dashboard-v2` (shared component), so B5 changes land on both.** **The `getDashboardReportSnapshot()` QUERY survives** — only the component was deleted; it still returns `{ latest }` (`LIMIT 1`; HO 159 dropped its `previousDates` field + the `.home-snapshot-prev*` CSS). **Shipped since (HO 283/286/365):** the WoW deltas, sparklines, and per-metric hover cards are all **built now** (this entry previously banked them). **Dropped (NOT built):** the `IN GOV-OPS` line (no honest trailing-7-day fit); event callouts (`stage_transitions` still thin). BREAKING (72h) is the top panel of the LEFT column. The treemap + funnel still drive `?stage=` / `?topics=` click-to-filter (HO 132 in-place rebase): MOVERS and BREAKING both rebase to the filtered slice; the topic treemap rebases when STAGE is selected; the funnel rebases when TOPIC is selected. `ActiveFilterStrip` shows the active filter with `× CLEAR` and `VIEW IN /bills →` links. `await searchParams` opts the route into dynamic rendering. **`DashboardTopicTreemap`** (HO 231, replaced `DashboardBubbleChart`): `"use client"` island using `d3-hierarchy::treemap` with a squarified tile layout, area = topic count (honest area encoding, unlike the old sqrt-radius bubbles), GOV-anchored, half-height; soft-nav via `router.push(href, { scroll: false })` on click pushing `?topics=`; per-topic fill from `lib/topic-colors.ts` with the HO 180 hover popover decoding the abbreviation. The HO 132.1 slide-out drawer was already dropped (rebase-in-place). `--home-header-height` is dead code (the no-scroll calc that used it is gone).
- `/` — **the dashboard.** HO 311 promoted the **approved 2-col redesign (HO 253)** from the parallel `/dashboard-v2` route to `/` (the old `/` is preserved at `/dashboard-classic`; `/dashboard-v2` now 308-redirects here). `export const dynamic = "force-dynamic"`. **Distributions click-to-filter (HO 320 — RESTORED; was `staticMode` under the HO 311 swap, now closed):** the page `await`s `searchParams` and threads `DashboardFilters` (`sanitizeStage`/`sanitizeTopic`) into the gated distributions, the MOVERS feed (`ActivityTicker variant="v2" filters={filters}`), and BREAKING — so clicking a `StageFunnel` bar / `DashboardTopicTreemap` cell pushes `?stage=`/`?topics=` to `/` and rebases that slice (cross-rebase: funnel rebases on TOPIC, treemap on STAGE), with `ActiveFilterStrip` (× CLEAR → `/`, VIEW IN /bills →). Distributions stay summary-gated — `getStageDistribution(filters, true)` / `getTopicDistribution(filters, true)` — so the gated-count agreement holds while filtered; the header's four stage segments use a SEPARATE corpus-wide `getStageDistribution(undefined, true)` so the masthead doesn't rebase. TOP STALLS / NEW THIS WEEK stay corpus-wide (classic parity — those feed queries don't take `DashboardFilters`). v2's body description follows (it carried over unchanged): **`DashboardV2Header` (HO 253)** is a RESTACK of `HomeHeader` reusing its classes: the breadcrumb masthead + HO 244-style stat readout (corpus numbers passed IN, **summary-gated** so v2's "tracked" total agrees with the inner pages it links to — fetched once via `getCorpusStats(true)` / `getStageDistribution(undefined,true)` / `getTopicDistribution(undefined,true)`), the LAST SYNC subhead, the **two-tape stack** (MARKETS over ODDS — relabelled + expanded by the B2 arc HO 289–294, see Markets tape), then nav. Body order: **(1) `<CompetitiveRacesBlock showBattlefield variant="v2" />`** — the COMPETITIVE tab carries the **D↔R battlefield axis (`Battlefield`, HO 254)** above the **rich race cards (HO 260)**; **(2) `<WeeklyBand />`**; **(3) a 49/51 two-column body** — LEFT: `BreakingNewsBlock` over the tabbed `DistributionsTabs` (StageFunnel | DashboardTopicTreemap, gated); RIGHT: `ActivityTabs` with THREE tabs **MOVERS (`ActivityTicker variant="v2"`) / TOP STALLS (`TopStalls variant="v2"`) / NEW THIS WEEK (`NewThisWeek variant="v2"`, HO 249)** — the v2 feed rows + rich expand are `V2FeedList` (HO 257, matching the mock's MOVERS box; `/dashboard-classic`'s feed keeps the old `BillRowList`/`TopStallsList`). **`Battlefield` (HO 254):** server component, a single-row lean axis (`getBattlefieldSeats`, competitive band `|consensus|≤1.5`) — featured/card seats as labeled dots, the rest rolled into lean-tier aggregate ticks with hover popovers; markers carry `data-seat={raceId}` for the HO 260 cross-highlight. **Rich race cards (HO 260):** `CompetitiveRacesStrip variant="v2"` renders `RaceCard` (the mock's `.race-card`) for the 4 competitive seats — incumbent + tenure + INCUMBENT/OPEN tag, the D↔R spread bar (rater dots + band + ◇ Kalshi / ◆ Polymarket diamonds + divergence chip, math in `lib/race-spread.ts`), rater pills, and the WAR CHEST | KALSHI | POLYMARKET stat row (Senate 3 cells incl. Polymarket; House 2 cells + 2024 margin). `RaceCrossHighlight` (client) wires card↔battlefield-marker `.hl` on `data-seat`. The cards read `getRacesIndex(cycle)` rich rows (incumbent join + cash + margin + 3 ratings + Kalshi + `polymarketOdds`). `/dashboard-classic`'s `CompetitiveRacesBlock` (default variant) keeps its 2×2 hover-popover cards. **HO 274 — the rich cards' Kalshi + Polymarket odds render as PARTY LEAN, not candidate name, so the K/P pair is directly comparable.** `RaceCard` resolves a candidate-named market to a party via the seat's FULL candidate roster (the prefetched hub candidates, threaded in from `CompetitiveRacesStrip`), NOT the incumbent alone — incumbent-only was the bug that left a challenger market (ME "Platner", NJ-07 "Bennett") showing a surname beside the other venue's party. Unresolvable favorites keep the candidate name (the honest fallback); House seats with no Polymarket collapse to the Kalshi cell (no dangling column). **Battlefield markers AND the card's candidate dot both color from the seat's incumbent party** (`getBattlefieldSeats.incumbentParty` = `members.party` via the incumbent join → `partyColor(...)`), keeping the two surfaces consistent — marker POSITION is rating lean, so a red incumbent marker can sit toward the D side (ME-SEN); expected, not a bug (see oddities.md).

- `/welcome` — **the landing (HO 361, B1 / last leg of the multi-user arc; the live MOVERS+tape upgrade is folded in).** Split-layout marketing page owned by `app/welcome/page.tsx` (`landing.module.css`), built from the signed-off mock `docs/design/landing.html`, with **no masthead / `HeaderBar`** of its own. **Routing is a cookie redirect from `/`, NO middleware** (A1 deliberately added none): `app/page.tsx` bounces an anonymous visitor with no **`ct_seen`** cookie to `/welcome`; the landing's **Enter terminal** button (`LandingCTAs`, the only client JS) sets `ct_seen` + routes to `/`, while **Sign in** calls `signIn("github", { callbackUrl: "/" })`. A returning cookie OR a session renders the terminal directly, so neither path loops. **The live panel is REAL, not a static replica** (corrects the early-mock framing): the MOVERS rows (`getStageChanges`), the readout stats (`getCorpusStats`/`getStageDistribution`), and the markets tape (`getLatestMarketTicks`) all read the **same cached Turso queries `/` serves** — reuse, not recompute — rendered in the mock's compact markup (no star/expand/media column), **NOT** the live `BillRow`/`MarketsTape` components. **Only the BREAKING strip is invented** — a rotating evergreen flavor ticker (`BreakingTicker`; the deadpan red `BREAKING` tag is the joke). Chip colors come live from `topic-colors.ts`. `force-dynamic`.
- `/bills` — unified BILLS|NEWS feed (HO 151 restructured; **route renamed `/feed` → `/bills` in HO 184** to match its identity — `/feed` 308-redirects in `next.config.ts` with the query string preserved, so bookmarks/deployed URL survive; the GROUP_TABS group key stays `"feed"` internally so `pathToNavKey` is unaffected, with an explicit `pathToNavKey("/bills") → "feed"` matcher added since `/bills` no longer has a sub-nav tab — see the double-nav note below). **HO 185 removed the per-page `page-masthead` H1** (`Bills:\>`/`News:\>`); the unified breadcrumb path is now the only masthead and tracks the toggle — `Congressional Terminal:\119TH\Bills>_` in bills mode, `…\News>_` in news mode (the `mode`/`presidentAlias` props on `HeaderBar` drive the segment, server-side). A single `SegmentedToggle` (`?mode=bills`|`?mode=news`, default bills) swaps the filter bar, row component, and count chrome; page resets on every filter or mode change. Per-mode params don't collide; the other mode's params persist in the URL across switches (no aggressive clear). `BILLS` (`?mode=bills`): **25/page** (`FEED_PAGE_SIZE`, HO 187 — down from 100, not the 50 this entry long claimed), `BillRowList` accordions (HO 148). **HO 187/189 restructured inner pages into 4 chrome bands** (see the HeaderBar / inner-chrome note): (1) the title bar (path + inline filter-aware sync + nav), (2) the **control strip** — BILLS|NEWS toggle + `StageFilter` (ALL STAGES, includes `president`) + chamber `SegmentedToggle` (ALL/HOUSE/SENATE) + a **compact ⌕ `SearchBox`** (`flex:1`, max 230px) + **INCLUDE CEREMONIAL** + `SortDropdown` pinned right (search + ceremonial moved here out of the old HeaderBar masthead), (3) the **topics band** — the feed sub-nav Changes·President·Reports + a divider rule + the multi-select `TopicFilter` chips (comma-list `?topics=…`), (4) the **legend + pagination** band (`StageLegend` + `Pagination`). The markets tape was removed from inner pages in HO 187, then **restored app-wide in HO 202, then collapsed to a single line in HO 234** (one `<MarketsTape />` mounted once in `HeaderBar` below the title bar, so it's on `/bills` and every inner page). BILLS-only params: `stage`, `sponsor`, `chamber`, `ceremonial`, `cluster`, `q`, `topics`, `sort`. The only structurally shared param is `page`; `topics`/`sort` are BILLS-only but preserved in the URL across a mode switch (round-trip symmetry), not consumed by NEWS rendering. (Corrected in the HO 160 sweep — the prior "shared `topics`/`sort`/`page`" framing conflated URL-preservation with cross-mode use.) `NEWS` (`?mode=news`): 50/page, `NewsRow` list inside the same `news-header-row` chrome the standalone `/news` used, `NewsFilters` chips for `SOURCE` (politico/the_hill/roll_call) + `WINDOW` (24/72/168/720h, default 72h) + single-select `TOPIC` (`?topic=…` singular, distinct from BILLS' plural) + a clearable `?bill=<id>` pill that scopes to one bill (drops window + confidence gate while scoped — same as HO 130's per-bill semantics). NEWS-only params: `source`, `topic`, `window`, `bill`. SORT is a static "most recent" label — no dropdown shell. `HeaderBar` runs in `pageTitle="News mentions"` + `pageCount=mentions` mode for NEWS, dropping the search box. Backed by `getNewsFeed({source?, topic?, windowHours?, billId?, page?, pageSize?})` which reuses `getBreakingNewsForHome`'s dedup-by-article-key + confidence floor (0.7) when not bill-scoped, paginates via OFFSET, tag `news-breaking`. Companion sanitizers: `sanitizeNewsSource`, `sanitizeWindowHours`. **President desk-time alias:** `/president` is now its **own in-surface page** (HO 359 — see its entry; it no longer redirects here), but the `/bills?stage=president` alias path described here still applies for direct visits/power filtering — when `stage=president` is the sole active stage AND no explicit `?sort` override, the feed page re-applies the legacy `daysSinceMode="desk-time"` desk-time column AND switches the SQL `ORDER BY` to ASC (oldest-at-desk first) — the column and the order ship together so the visible signal stays coherent. `FeedFilters.direction?: "asc"` carries this through `getFeedBills`; it's internal-only, never written by URL params and never surfaced in `SortDropdown`. `getPresidentBills` / `getPresidentCount` were deleted in HO 154.1 as orphans of this redirect. **News alias absorbed:** `/news` redirects to `/bills?mode=news` (and `/news?bill=<id>` to `/bills?mode=news&bill=<id>`); `MediaAttentionCell` points directly at the new target. (The `/news` + `/president` alias `redirect()`s were retargeted straight to `/bills` in HO 184 to avoid a `/news → /feed → /bills` double-hop.) **Double-nav resolved (HO 184):** the BILLS|NEWS `SegmentedToggle` is the canonical mode switch; the `feed` GROUP_TABS row previously *also* carried Bills + News tabs (a redundant second way to switch the same mode), so they were dropped — the feed sub-nav now reads **Changes · President · Reports** (sibling/derived views; Reports kept as a deliberate pre-existing special-case). Accepted tradeoff: in bills/news mode no sub-nav tab is active.
- `/bill/[id]` — detail page (card panel layout). HO 145 added a **Committees** block between the field grid (Sponsor/Introduced/Last action/Stage/Topics) and the Summary, fed by `getBillCommittees(billId)`. Section is **skipped entirely** when the bill has no committee_bills rows (a normal state for fresh introductions / many resolutions — a "no referrals" line would be noise). Each row links to `/committee/[systemCode]`, carries the chamber label, an `↳ ParentName` caption for subcommittees, and an `Activity · Xmo ago` suffix via `formatRelativeAgeLong`. No dedupe — a referred-then-reported sequence shows two rows. **HO 440 added a LOBBYING section** (after Hearings, before Summary), fed by `getBillLobbying(billId)`: top firms / top clients ranked by **distinct filings**, reusing `FilingRow` + the extracted `LobbyingMiniBars` (consistent with the `/lobbying` per-code drill). **Omitted entirely on zero-link bills** — null-safe absence like the Committees section (`getBillLobbying` returns null → no section, never a 500; the blob/live/zero-link branches were all prod-verified at `42ff9c0`).
- `/watchlist` — bills flagged via `★ Watch`
- `/stale` — **stage-led "past committee" stalls (HO 350, supersedes the old oldest-first-all-stages view).** Default scope is the **past-committee group `stage IN ('floor','other_chamber','president')`** (`STALE_PAST_COMMITTEE_STAGES`, enacted excluded — success isn't a stall), still gated to **60+ days** since last action (`STALE_DAYS=60`), sorted **legislative-stage DESC then furthest-action-first** (`latest_action_date ASC`). So the surface answers "what advanced past committee and then went quiet, ordered by how far it got," not "every old bill oldest-first." The header reads `past committee · stalled 60+ days · furthest first`. **Stage filter** (`STALE_FILTER_STAGES` = `introduced`/`committee`/`floor`/`other_chamber`; `president`/`enacted` not offered) lets you isolate a single stage — picking one drops the default past-committee scope and shows just that stage (the index/sort flips accordingly; see the `getStaleBills` helper). A **committee-backlog footer** (`getStaleCommitteeCount`) renders `{N} more sit in committee →` linking to `?stage=committee` — the committee wall is one click away, not the default. **Procedural-housekeeping filter (HO 350, `lib/stale-procedural.ts`):** the default view hides one-time opening-week organizational resolutions (they did their job — not stalls). It's a curated hybrid: a **FROZEN id list** `STALE_PROCEDURAL_IDS` (13 items — electoral-vote count, elect/notify officers, fix meeting hour, quorum/assemble, pro-tem election, **including the 3 joint-session resolutions** `hconres-11/16/74`) + a **LIVE title pattern** `STALE_PROCEDURAL_TITLE_PATTERN = "electing members%"` (anchored, for the recurring "Electing Members to … committees" family) + a **blocklist** `STALE_PROCEDURAL_BLOCKLIST` (`119-hres-966`, `119-sres-6` — honoring/thanks resolutions that mention "President pro tempore" and must survive the pattern). The boundary: `hres-5` (the Rules package) and "Amending the Rules" resolutions are **never** filtered — they're real, and the anchored `electing members%` pattern can't catch them. An **INCLUDE PROCEDURAL** toggle (`ProceduralToggle`, `?procedural=1`) is the escape hatch that reveals them in one click — also the safety valve if the curation ever grabs a real bill. To extend, edit the three lists in `lib/stale-procedural.ts` (validated by `scripts/diagnostic/stale-procedural-350.ts`; signed off before the default shipped). Same filter chrome as the feed (topics/chamber/search/ceremonial). Action column renders days-since (`247d`) instead of a date, color-coded by threshold (`daysSinceMode="staleness"`).
- `/president` — **HO 359: a real in-surface page** (the president's-desk sub-tab), no longer the HO 151 redirect to `/bills?stage=president`. Clicking PRESIDENT in the feed sub-nav used to dump the user onto the full `/bills` feed (sub-nav unmarked, breadcrumb under Bills); now `app/president/page.tsx` carries the **same chrome as `/changes`** (its sibling) — `HeaderBar` + the feed `GroupTabs` sub-nav (Changes · President · Reports, with the **active tab marked**) + `StageLegend` + `BillRowList` — so the tab keeps you in-surface. Data is unchanged: president-stage bills, oldest-at-desk-first (`direction:"asc"`, racing the 10-day veto clock) with the `daysSinceMode="desk-time"` days-since column — the exact semantics the `/bills?stage=president` alias still applies for direct visits / power filtering. Breadcrumb `Bills\President` (`lib/breadcrumb.ts`).
- `/changes` — bills whose stage moved in the last 7 days, sorted by `stage_changed_at DESC` (the `getStageChanges` predicate). The "in motion" view between `/stale` and `/president`. No stage filter (the page is about transitions, not destinations). Topic + search + chamber filters only. **The page renders standard `BillRowList` rows.** The from→to transition-render idiom — the `▸ INTRO → ▸▸ COMMITTEE` glyph with the prior stage dimmed via a `muted` `StageIndicator`, the `Xd ago`-from-`stage_changed_at` column, the `.changes-feed` wider-stage wrapper, and `BillRow`'s `showStageTransition` opt-in — **was removed around HO 125/148/191 and no longer exists**; `BillRow` has no `previous_stage`/transition rendering today. (This is the same idiom HO 232 found gone when it scoped the MOVERS tab.) Empty state: `No stage changes in the last 7 days.`
- `/members` — **the merged Members + Committees two-pane browser (HO 328 — replaced the HO 152/196/197 ranked-list-with-scatters page; the committee index folded in from the now-redirected `/committees`).** A committee rail (~312px, `getCommitteesIndex`) on the left + a member list (`1fr`) on the right. **Two ideology surfaces mount above the browser:** the HO 425 `IdeologyStrip` dotplot, and — new at **HO 428** — `PolarizationOverTime` **collapsed by default** at the very top (a ~384px over-time chart that shouldn't bury the browser; its chamber toggle inits to the page chamber — House when ALL — then toggles independently, fed `getPolarizationHistory()` + `getPolarizationBand()` from the page `Promise.all`). The **chamber** filter drives BOTH panes; **party/state/sort/ceremonial/search** drive the member list only. Members are still aggregated from `bills` (lineage HOs 67/89/152), now beside the rail. Filter bar (full-width strip): the `MEMBERS` title + `{total} of the 119th` count + ALL/HOUSE/SENATE `SegmentedToggle` + `PartyFilter` (R/D/I) + `StateFilter` + VOLUME/PASS RATE `SegmentedToggle` (`?sort=volume|passrate`, `getMembersRanked` ORDER BY swap) + **INCLUDE CEREMONIAL** (`CeremonialToggle`, `billsAggCte(includeCeremonial)` shifts the totals/ranking) + a member `SearchBox`. **LEFT RAIL** (`getCommitteesIndex({chamber})`): an **UPCOMING HEARINGS** group pinned at the top (`getUpcomingForRail` → `getUpcomingMeetings({days:7, chamber})`, soonest-per-committee, `◷ N THIS WEEK` in the header) — **UPCOMING, not LIVE NOW** (the schema has no in-progress / end-time signal + the page is daily-cached, so "in session now" can't be derived honestly; see oddities + the stale mock), then `CommitteeRailRow` rows (chamber tag, member count, activity bar scaled to `railMax = max(recentBillCount)`). Clicking a committee **scopes the roster**: `?committee=<systemCode>` → `getCommitteeRoster(code, sort, includeCeremonial)` (chair → ranking → volume order), and the per-member bar **rescales to the roster max** (vs the global filtered max unscoped). A scoped context header (`mc-ctx`) carries the committee name + `committee detail →` + `× all members`. When a member is expanded, the rail marks the committees they sit on (lighter-amber `●`, `onMarker`) and the header shows `· ● on N` (those that appear in the rail) via `getMemberCommittees`. **RIGHT PANE**: a topic key strip (the union of on-screen topics, most-common-first, the legend for what's rendered), the column header (`MEMBER · BILLS·TOPIC MIX · RATE · ENACT · BILLS`), then the member rows. Each row = member name + party-colored `[party-state]` bracket + `PalestineBadge` (when scored) + a **`MemberTopicBar`** (top-3 topics + `OTHR` rollup; segment widths from the member's topic counts, colors from `lib/topic-colors`; **total length scaled to `pageMax`** — global filtered max unscoped / roster max scoped, so a bar means different things in the two states, see oddities) + RATE (green >0 / dim at 0) · ENACT (`N ✓`) · BILLS figures. The full ranked list is **unpaginated** (`LIST_LIMIT = 600` covers all 536 current members, scrolls on overflow) so the bar scales to the true global max; scoped rosters cap at `ROSTER_CAP = 10` with the rest behind a `RosterShowAll` disclosure. Topic-mix data is `getMembersTopicMix(includeCeremonial)` — a **flat** array (`json_each` fanout, grouped per-member in the page, cached tag `bills`, forced onto `idx_bills_sponsor_topics`). **New helpers:** `getMembersTopicMix`, `getCommitteeRoster`. **New components:** `MemberTopicBar` (server), `CommitteeRailRow` + `RosterShowAll` (client islands). The HO 152/197 `MemberProductivityScatter` pair and the HO 196 one-bar-per-sort/green-track list were **dropped** in the merge; their query `getSponsorProductivity` (+ `SponsorProductivityRow`) is **deleted (HO 328)**. Click any row to inline-expand (`?expanded=<bioguide_id>`, URL-driven single-open, `<Link replace scroll={false}>`) a `SponsorExpandedPanel` with `committeeCap={Infinity}` (uncapped COMMITTEES), fed by the 5-query `Promise.all` (`getSponsorStats` / `getSponsorTopTopics` / `getSponsorRecentBills` / `getMemberCommittees` / `getMemberAffiliations`) — **HO 198/200 rebuilt it from the ~650px vertical stack into a ~280px 3-column card matching the HO 191 bill panel** (grid `210px · minmax(0,1.5fr) · minmax(0,1fr)`, `.sponsor-card-grid`/`-rail`/`-mid`/`-right`):
  - **LEFT RAIL:** 96px photo (`SponsorPhoto` via a new `width` prop — hub stays 150px; bioguide-direct URL + `onError`→initials, **NOT** `depiction_url`, which the panel never had on its path) · `Sen./Rep. First Last` identity (new `chamber` prop threaded from `MemberRanking`) + party bracket + state · stat block (TOTAL BILLS / ENACTED n+%) · STAGES glyph run (`--stage-*`) · TOPICS chips · **CAUCUSES** folded under topics (HO 152, `getMemberAffiliations`/`CaucusBadge`, skip-on-empty) · **USCPR SCORECARD (HO 200)** — the shared `PalestineBadge` + `total_score` + `#rank of 47` for scored members, an explicit muted **"Not scored"** for off-sheet members (the honest gap — no fabricated/default grade; same idiom as the bill panel's "No related news"; third-party USCPR attribution mirrored from the list badge) · stacked VIEW DETAIL / OPEN IN FEED buttons. **The state flag was dropped.**
  - **MIDDLE:** RECENT BILLS · N total, capped to 7 + "SEE ALL N BILLS →"; titles `truncate pr-3`, the date `min-w-[58px] shrink-0 text-right` so titles ellipsis with clear space before a consistent date edge.
  - **RIGHT:** COMMITTEES · N (HO 152, `getMemberCommittees`) — **uncapped under the HO 328 merge** (`committeeCap={Infinity}`; was ~8 on the old page) + CHAIR/RANKING badges + `↳` subcommittees.
  - All three columns share ONE `--bg-row-hover` base with `border-right` dividers (the **seam fix** — earlier per-column `--bg-panel` rails read as a color seam against the lighter middle; the HO 191 panel stays one continuous surface the same way). Caps are render-only slices; the scorecard's `total_score` is the only added column (`getMembersRanked`, existing JOIN) — **no new queries**. URL-driven single-open via `?expanded=<bioguide_id>` (UNCHANGED; same pattern as the original HO 67 page; the `/bills` BillRowList's client-state model is the alternate idiom — reconciling the two expand mechanisms is HO 154 normalization, not here). The spec-7 data-quality "N issues" badge stays **deferred and never built** (no schema signal) — HO 198 confirmed there was nothing to remove.
- `/trades` — **corpus-wide member stock-trades index (HO 389).** A recency feed of `stock_trades` (`getRecentTrades({page, pageSize})`) rendered with the shared **`TradeRow`** (`showMember` ON — adds a leading member cell + the `.trade-row--with-member` grid variant, incl. its mobile fallback), paginated. Above it, a **most-traded-tickers** ranked-bar rollup (`getMostTradedTickers`, trailing 90d) — **unscoped view only**. **`?member=<bioguide>`** scopes to one member: canonical name in the H1, a back-link to the corpus view, rollup suppressed. **Breadcrumb nests under Members.** NULL-bioguide rows (unmatched FMP disclosures) render the raw disclosed name as plain text — never dropped. The member hub's **"View all N trades →"** is now a real `<Link>` to `/trades?member=<bioguide>` (was a dead `<span>`).
- `/patterns` — bill pattern visualization (HO 128; reframed HO 346–348). **The page H1 is `LEGISLATIVE PATTERNS` (HO 346)** with a `{matched} measures in {N} forms · out of {patternTotal} · {pct}%` meta line (live; denominator is the page's OWN matched + unmatched, NOT the corpus BILLS TRACKED figure — using the corpus count makes the % stop reconciling with the unmatched number) and a sans blurb ("The same forms of legislation, filed again and again. Click one to see the measures."). **Left column is `PatternBars` (HO 347, a server component — REPLACED the deleted `PatternBubbleSVG`):** a ranked horizontal bar list, one row per regex pattern from `lib/cluster-patterns.ts`, **bar length = bill count (linear, scaled to the max)**, **bar color = % past committee on the same `--text-dim` → `--stage-enacted` STALLED→MOVING ramp the bubbles used** (saturating at 30%), columns `Pattern · [bar] · Bills · % past`. It **absorbed the former standalone ALL PATTERNS table** (HO 347). Selection is URL-driven via `?selected=<slug>` (validated by `sanitizeClusterId`); each row is a plain `<Link>` pushing the param with `scroll: false` (no client island), and **a pattern is ALWAYS selected** — the page auto-selects the top (highest-count) pattern when the URL carries none, so the right column is never blank. `PatternLegend` renders the gradient strip below the bars. When selected, `PatternDrilldownPanel` renders below with a headline line `{N} bills · {X}% past committee · {K} enacted` — **NOTE: the per-bill `Y% ceremonial` figure was DROPPED from this strip (HO 348)** because it contradicts the form-based filler framing (below) — do not reintroduce it — plus a top-5 sponsor mini-bar-chart (party-colored, name-truncated) and a `[View all N bills in feed →]` link to `/bills?cluster=<slug>` (HO 51 drill-out convention). Right column shows the selected pattern's top-10 most-recent bills via reused `BillRow compact` with pre-resolved `getWatchedBillIds` membership. **Filler Watch strip (HO 348, `FillerWatchStrip` — a client island, collapsible):** sits between the meta line and the blurb. A `CEREMONIAL · NON-BINDING` summary row (`{filed} filed · {enacted} enacted · {pastCommittee} past committee · sponsors {D}%/{R}%`) that click-expands to an attrition row + a register line + a sponsor-split footer — **every number is live-interpolated from `getFillerWatch()`** (`filed`/`pastCommittee`/`enacted`/`nonBinding`/`d`/`r`/`i`), so the prose self-reconciles each sync and can never drift. Backed by `getClusterStats()` (extended with `pastCommittee/enacted/ceremonial`), `getClusterDrilldown(clusterId)`, and `getFillerWatch()`, all `unstable_cache` tagged `bills`. **HO 199:** the top-5-sponsors sub-query `GROUP BY sponsor_bioguide_id` (was `GROUP BY sponsor_name, sponsor_party`), keeping `MAX(sponsor_name)` for the "Last, First" shape. Mobile (`< 700px`): columns stack. Internal column (`bills.cluster_id`) and helper names keep `cluster*` naming per HO 114.
- `/lobbying` — **LDA lobbying surface, issue-code-first (HO 437).** A standalone analytical surface (the `/patterns` class); new top-level nav item (`pathToNavKey("/lobbying") → "lobbying"`, breadcrumb `Lobbying`, **8th nav item — `PrimaryNav` divider bumped 6→7**). `export const dynamic = "force-dynamic"`. **Sections:** (1) stat readout + sans blurb; (2) two-column (reusing `.patterns-layout`) — LEFT `IssueBars` (ranked bars, bar = filing count, native `general_issue_code` labels NOT crosswalked to the 24 CBT topics, URL-driven `?issue=<code>`, top code auto-selected) · RIGHT `IssueDrill` (headline counts + top-5 clients / top-5 firms mini-bars + recent, from `rollup.drill[code]`); (3) a **BY CBT TOPIC** section (HO 444) — the corpus re-bucketed into the 24 CBT topics via the static issue→topic map, topic-colored bars (`getTopicCrosswalk`, blob `lda_topic_crosswalk`; null → omitted), non-interactive v1, header labeled "by issue focus" (NOT "share of filings" — multi-code, non-partition); (4) a **TOP FIRMS** section (HO 442) — a registrant leaderboard by **distinct filings** (`getTopFirms`, blob `lda_top_firms`; null → omitted), native issue-code labels **NOT** CBT-topic-crosswalked, mobile drops the Top-issue + Bill-linked columns <640px; (5) corpus recent-filings feed (`FilingRow` + `Pagination`). **Bars + drill are BLOB-served** (`getLobbyingRollup`, precomputed — request-time + live-per-code were both ruled out >25s cold, oddities); **only the feed is live** (`getRecentFilings`, `MAX_FEED_PAGES=40`). `FilingRow` = `{age · registrant → client · issue chips · bill chips}`; bill chips deep-link to `/bill/[id]`, segment omitted when none (honest gap). Built with inline tokens (not the 4-col `.pattern-bar` grid) to avoid coupling to the concurrent session's live `globals.css`. Banked: bill-keyed **shipped HO 440** (`getBillLobbying`; see the `/bill/[id]` entry); top-firms leaderboard **shipped HO 442** (the TOP FIRMS section above, `getTopFirms`); the crosswalk **shipped HO 444** (the BY-CBT-TOPIC section, `getTopicCrosswalk`, blob `lda_topic_crosswalk`; native issue bars unchanged) — **nothing from the HO 437 block still banked.**

  **Filler framing (the durable convention).** The cumulative ceremonial / "filler" read on `/patterns` is **form-based** — the four ceremonial clusters (`awareness-designation`, `honoring-resolution`, `facility-naming`, `sense-of-congress`, `FILLER_WATCH_PATTERNS` in `lib/queries.ts`), with `nonBinding` = the three non-facility clusters (they cannot become law by nature; only facility namings can). This is **deliberately NOT** the per-bill `is_ceremonial` flag — and the per-bill "% ceremonial" stat was dropped from the Patterns detail strip (HO 348) precisely because the two framings contradict each other. **Do not reintroduce a per-bill % ceremonial figure on `/patterns`.** Separately, the **dashboard `WeeklyBand` filler-share bar (HO 351) uses a BROAD definition** — `is_ceremonial = 1 OR cluster_id IN (the four)` (`getWeeklyBandFiller`) — so the dashboard and Patterns numbers are intentionally computed differently; that's expected, not drift.
- `/reports` — index of weekly reports, newest first (handoff 75, redesigned HO 153). `HeaderBar` runs in `pageTitle="Weekly Reports"` + `pageCount` mode (nav + count chrome). **HO 185 removed the per-page `Reports:\>` sub-masthead** — and with it the whole HO 154.4 `<TerminalPrompt>` / `.page-masthead` pattern that every list page (`/bills`, `/watchlist`, `/changes`, `/stale`, `/members`, `/committees`, `/patterns`, `/trends`, `/races`, `/primaries`) used to render below GroupTabs. The section name now lives once in the unified breadcrumb path (`…\Reports>_`), so these list pages render just `GroupTabs` + content. `.report-row` grid is `110px 1fr 70px`: amber-mono week-start date, a two-line body (`Weekly Report` title + 1-line derived lead excerpt indented under it), then a muted `read →` chip that lights amber-bright on hover. **HO 242 added a per-row stats strip** to the body (`ReportRow.tsx`): `Laws N · Intro N · Moves N` (bills enacted / non-ceremonial introductions / stage-changes that week, `tabular-nums`) — hidden on NULL (un-backfilled) rows. **Note the deviation:** the handoff framed this as a *top* stat strip; it shipped as a **per-row** strip instead — there's no cross-week aggregate strip above the list (the `Productivity vs. the 118th` chart is the only above-list element). Lead text is the report's first prose paragraph between the H1 and the first `##` section, markdown-noise stripped and clamped to ~180 chars via `extractReportLead(content_md)` in `lib/report-lead.ts` — derived at read time, never stored, per spec 6 / HO 153 ("don't add a field to the generation pipeline for a display concern"). Click navigates to `/reports/[slug]`. Pagination via `?page=N` at `PAGE_SIZE = 20`. Empty state: `Reports begin Monday <next Monday>.` Backed by `getReportsWithLead(limit, offset)` (HO 242 extended it to project `laws_count`/`intro_count`/`moves_count` → `lawsCount`/`introCount`/`movesCount`; backfilled by `scripts/backfill-report-counts.ts`); count via `getReportCount`. The pre-HO-153 lightweight `getReports` / `getReportsList` helpers were removed in HO 154.1. Cached tag `reports`, 1h revalidate; the report cron's `revalidateTag('reports')` flushes all three. Global nav includes `⎘ Reports` as its own top-level item (HO 150). The `Productivity vs. the 118th` `LawsEnactedComparison` chart stays above the list — untouched by HO 153.
- `/reports/[slug]` — individual weekly report. Markdown body rendered by `components/ReportMarkdown.tsx` (react-markdown + remark-gfm) with terminal-aesthetic component overrides for h1/h2/p/ul/li/code/table/em/strong. `[Download .md ↓]` link in the header pulls from `/reports/[slug]/download`, which serves `report.content_md` with `Content-Disposition: attachment; filename="cbt-${slug}.md"`. Unknown slug renders a friendly empty state with a back link, not Next's `notFound()`.
- `/members/[bioguideId]` — member hub (handoff 60, +61, +62, +77, +80). Photo (depiction_url, plain `<img>` with initials fallback), name, party + state + district chip, born year, next-election chip (links to `/race/<id>` when the member has a non-null `next_election_year` — handoff 62), and the top-2 caucus badges by priority appended to the meta line (handoff 61), and — for Senate Democrats only — the USCPR Palestine scorecard letter grade as a `PalestineBadge` chip at the end of the meta line (handoff 138, extended to the `/members` row list in handoff 142). Grade-to-color is three tiers: A/B render in `--text-secondary` (covered, not flagged), C in `--accent-amber`, D/F in `--vote-nay` (alarm; rose rather than `--party-republican` to avoid cross-wiring with the party dot on a Dem header). Source attribution lives in the tooltip (`USCPR Palestine scorecard: F (rank #3 of 47)`), never on the visible chip. **Surfaces:** hub header (`/members/[bioguideId]`) + `/members` row list, inline after the name in the row's name cell. HO 138's original "hub-only" scope was reversed by HO 142 after Corey saw the hub badge live and wanted the same chip on the roster — the visual-asymmetry concern (47 of 535 members get badged) was acceptable in practice. Still kept off `BillRow` sponsor expansion; separate scope if it comes up. Absence of badge is the correct signal (no "—"/"N/A" placeholder). The `/members` query (`getMembersRanked`) extends with a `LEFT JOIN palestine_scorecard` projecting `grade` + `rank` + (HO 200) `total_score` (→ `MemberRanking.palestineScore`, for the expanded-card scorecard detail). The full PALESTINE SCORECARD section from HO 90 stays put further down the hub page; the chip just elevates the grade to glance level. Stat block (bills sponsored, enacted with %, avg cosponsor count). Affiliations row below stats renders every caucus badge by priority; absent entirely for unaffiliated members (no "Coming soon"). Top 10 sponsored bills via reused `BillRow` (no expand, no daysSinceMode). `[View all N bills →]` links to `/bills?sponsor=<bioguide_id>`. **Voting record section** (handoffs 77 + 80): a `MemberVoteStats` summary line (`House votes · N total · yea% · nay% · missed%` — chamber label flips for Senate members) plus the most-recent votes rendered by `MemberVoteRow`. `getMemberVotes` has no chamber filter; a senator's page shows their Senate votes and a House rep's page shows House votes purely because they have no `member_votes` rows in the other chamber. Empty state: `No {chamber} votes recorded for this member yet.` Stock-trades block sits below the voting section. Unknown bioguide_id renders a friendly empty state, not Next's `notFound()`. Reads from `members` + `affiliations` + `votes`/`member_votes` + `stock_trades`; refresh via `npm run sync:members`, `npm run seed:affiliations`, `npm run sync:votes`, `npm run sync:senate-votes`. HO 145 added a **Committees** section between Sponsored Bills and Voting Record, fed by `getMemberCommittees(bioguideId)`. Each row links to `/committee/[systemCode]`, shows chamber + committee type, prefixes subcommittees with `↳` and an inline `· Parent` caption, and renders a `CHAIR` (amber) or `RANKING` (muted) badge when `cm.role` matches — Vice/Co/Acting all collapse into the CHAIR badge; the raw role string lives in the row title attribute. Empty state: single muted `No committee assignments on file.` line (the assumption is every current member has at least one — empty = freshman whose YAML hasn't been published yet, or Speaker who doesn't sit on committees by tradition; both worth surfacing).
- `/committees` — **`redirect("/members")` as of HO 328.** The standalone committee index was folded into the `/members` LEFT RAIL (`getCommitteesIndex` powers both); the route now just redirects so old bookmarks resolve. `getCommitteesIndex` + its sanitizers (`sanitizeCommitteeChamber`/`sanitizeCommitteeSort`) live on as the rail's data layer. - `/committee/[systemCode]` — committee detail (HO 144 + HO 146). Header card: name, chamber, type, parent-committee link if `parent_system_code IS NOT NULL`, subcommittees roster (flat — no nesting in v1), retired badge if `is_current = 0`. HO 146 added a two-chart strip between the header card and the members/recent-bills grid: **`CommitteeActivityChart`** (left, ~60%) — stacked monthly bars over the current Congress, bars segmented by 4-bucket `activity_type` collapse (Referred/Markup/Reported/Other), throughput-funnel color mapping (`--stage-committee` → `--stage-floor` → `--stage-enacted` → `--text-dim`); legend chips only render for buckets present in the data; renders muted `Not enough activity to chart.` when the committee has fewer than 5 activity rows; SVG idiom forked from `BillsTimeSeries` (`CHART_HEIGHT=240`, `VB_WIDTH=1000`, same `PAD`, same `SvgGridY` + `SvgLegend`). **`CommitteeTopicDistribution`** (right, ~40%) — single-column horizontal bars, topic colors from `lib/topic-colors`, top-8 + Other rollup, reuses the `.topic-chamber-row` grid styling from `TopicMixByChamber`; renders muted `Topic data sparse for this committee.` when total non-ceremonial topic-tagged bills < 5. Both feed off the HO 146 helpers (`getCommitteeActivityByPeriod`, `getCommitteeTopicMix`) — see the helpers entry for the `LOWER()` normalization that handles the `committee_bills.activity_type` case-duplicate. Hearings/meetings, subcommittee rollup grouping, and hover tooltips are explicitly out of scope (deferred). Two body sections side-by-side on desktop (`md:grid-cols-[2fr_3fr]`), stacked on mobile: **Members** (left, ~40%) and **Recent activity** (right, ~60%). Members are reordered in TS to majority → minority → unside; within each block the row order already comes off `getCommitteeMembers` as `party_side ASC, rank ASC NULLS LAST` so chair/ranking float to the top. Chair/ranking rows render in `--accent-amber`; everyone else in `--text-primary`. Recent bills come from `getCommitteeBills(systemCode, 25, 30)` — the helper now takes an optional `sinceDays` arg and returns `CommitteeBillRow[]` (`{ bill: FeedBill; activityType; activityDate }`) so the page can show the per-committee activity caption (`Referred to · 3d ago`, computed via `daysSince`) immediately above each `BillRow` rather than the global `latest_action_*` line the row already carries. Each bill is rendered as **two sibling `<li>` elements** under the section's `<ul>`: an `ActivityCaption` muted-uppercase line first, then a compact `BillRow`. Two-li-per-row is HTML-valid (the `ul` content model is "zero or more li"). `BillRow` is used `compact` with the page-resolved `watchedSet` so the star renders correctly without a per-row fetch. Empty states for both sections are single muted lines, not full empty chrome (a quiet committee like `hspw12` Highways and Transit shows "No bills with committee activity in the last 30 days."). Unknown `systemCode` renders a friendly empty state with a back link, not `notFound()`. Cached at the query layer under tag `committees`.

Unknown id renders a friendly empty state, not Next's `notFound()`. Reads from `races` + `race_candidates` + (incumbent) `members`. - `/primaries` — **`permanentRedirect("/electoral")` as of HO 333.** The primary calendar is now the timeline band on the consolidated Electoral surface (see `/electoral`); the standalone recency-map page + its district modal/scrubber (HO 226 `PrimariesMap`/`PrimaryDistrictModal`) are superseded and left unreferenced (backlog open loop). The pre-HO-333 description follows (historical). 2026 primary + runoff calendar (HOs 91-96/107/120; redesigned HO 203). Server page; `GroupTabs` (the **`races` electoral group** as of HO 173 — sub-strip Races · Primaries; lights the Races top-nav tab, not Members); the per-page `TerminalPrompt` masthead was removed in HO 185 (see `/reports`). **No filter params** — it loads `getUpcomingPrimaries(600)` + `getPastPrimaries(600)` into **one date-sorted list (HO 208)**: voted primaries first (past `DESC`, most-recent results at the very top), a subtle `— Upcoming · not yet voted —` seam, then upcoming (`ASC`, nearest-first). The old two-section Upcoming / collapsed-Past `<details>` was **removed in HO 208** so the result bars are the first thing visible with no expand; the 300 cap was lifted to 600 to cover the full cycle (~457 past / ~447 upcoming). There's no `?chamber`/`?party`/`?page` (the entry that claimed those + a `PrimaryCalendarRow` was stale — neither exists). **HO 203 chrome:** passes `cursorAtEnd` + `liftSyncContrast` (matching Members/Races) — breadcrumb `Congressional Terminal:\119TH\Races\Primaries>`, cursor trailing the full sync, run `--text-muted` + count `--text-secondary`. No `search bills…` band to drop (bare `HeaderBar`, no `feedFilters`), so no `pageOwnsControls` migration. **Row (`PrimaryRow`, a client island; HO 203 → 207):** voted primaries (any candidate `vote_pct` non-NULL) render a **party-tinted results share bar** (HO 207) — top-3 by share + a `--border-strong` "+N" remainder, leader-bright → trailing-dim (`color-mix` toward `--bg-base`), 1px `--bg-base` hairline between segments (see the same-hue-bar design rule), `shrink-0`+`minWidth:0` so width tracks `vote_pct` exactly, inline `Name NN%`. Un-voted primaries render a **candidate-field fallback list** — incumbent-first, top-3 + "+N", labeled "— not yet voted" (**never a fake even-split bar** — an even split reads as "tied"). Empty rosters show muted "roster pending". **★ = advancer (the HO 207 reframe):** ★ marks every candidate who **won / advanced** (`status='winner'`) — runoffs advance two, so **two ★s is valid and expected** (TX-Sen R = Cornyn 42% + Paxton 40.5% both ★; `backfill:primary-results` writes `status` alongside `vote_pct`). The **seat incumbent** is a *separate* cue (amber name in the fallback list, an `INC` badge in the expand) so it never collides with ★ on one glyph. It's still resolved via the `seat_incumbent_bioguide` subquery in `PRIMARY_SELECT` (current House officeholder matched by `state`+`district`, `is_current`; falls back to the raw `incumbent` flag where unresolved — at-large/senate/open, ≤1 there), which drives the `INC` badge + the `/members/[bioguideId]` links, **not** ★. That subquery beats `races.incumbent_bioguide_id` (whose `primaries.race_id` link is dead 3/907, with cycle gaps + at-large excluded). The raw `primary_candidates.incumbent` flag ("is a sitting member of Congress") still drives the member link and legitimately flags >1 candidate in top-two/redraw contests (CA-40: Calvert+Kim; TX-18: Menefee+Green). **HO 148 click-to-expand, single-open** via a shared `PrimaryExpandProvider` context (client-side — wraps the whole list so it survives any native collapse): full candidate field with per-candidate **share % + advancer ★ + `INC` badge + `/members/[bioguideId]` links** (NO photos — separate future decision). The share bar was specced at HO 203, deferred while `vote_pct` was 100% NULL, unblocked by HO 206, and **shipped at HO 207** (results share, not polling — no polling model exists). **Voted-block guard (HO 208):** past contests with no roster AND no result are hidden from the voted block — a DISPLAY guard over two unfixed data problems (see the primaries data-debt note under "Things to watch for"); the clean page is **not** clean data. Reads `primaries` + `primary_candidates` (see "Runoff tracking" + the primaries cron notes). **Map-first as of HO 210:** the same `geoAlbersUsa` `CartogramShell` (PRIMARIES variant — VOTED/SOON/LATER recency bands) renders above this list as the default view, the date-sorted list one MAP/LIST toggle away; the pinned state card reuses the HO 207 `ShareBar` for voted contests and a `SCHEDULED · <full date>` list for unvoted. The shared shell, server-only geometry (`lib/us-map-geo.ts`), the two-coloring DO-NOT-UNIFY discipline, and the SOON rolling-window + VOTED-precedence are all documented under the `/races` entry. **District modal (HO 226 — sibling of the HO 225 Races modal):** `/primaries` wraps `CartogramShell` in **`PrimariesMap`** (mirror of `RacesMap`) holding modal state + the month scrubber; reuses the HO 225 `onStatePick` prop. **Three minimal, variant-scoped CartogramShell touches** (all behind `variant==="primaries"` / the optional `dimmedStates` prop so a `/races` render hits none — verified: races map renders 0 `opacity` attrs, purple fills, no `●` labels): (1) `primariesFill` recolored to deeper recency bands `VOTED #0e7490 / SOON #b45309 / LATER #1e2740 / NONE #11161f`; (2) a `● N` badge in the state label for multi-primary states (`cell.count` = contest count, set in `buildPrimariesCartogram`); (3) the optional `dimmedStates` prop dims states outside the scrubber month (opacity 0.28). **Month scrubber** (`PrimaryScrubber`, exported from `PrimaryDistrictModal`) = static segments `MAR·JUN·AUG·SEP·ALL`, no motion; `PrimariesMap` derives each state's month from its MAX `primary_date` and dims the rest. **`PrimaryDistrictModal`** reuses the HO 225 shell (`.rdm-*`) + the cached `/api/races/district-geo/[state]` route (geometry is chamber-agnostic, shared with Races); pick chips + map districts are keyed by `raceId` = the district seatId (`{ST}-{DD}-2026` house / `S-{ST}-2026` senate, set on each primaries `CartogramContest` so a polygon groups its D + R primaries).
